***батька.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:батька.html>ба́тька</a> (15915)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батя.html>ба́тя</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bátja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally a diminutive. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ба́тько</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bátʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">ба́цька</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bácʹka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батька.html>ба́тька</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bátʹka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батька.html>ба́тьки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батька.html>ба́тьки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батька.html>ба́тек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> father, dad
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>ле́зь</a> поперёд <a href = vnd.unilang:батька.html>ба́тьки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пекло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne lezʹ poperjód batʹki v peklo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't jump the gun; haste makes waste</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> "father", boss, master, lord, kingpin, number one, pro</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a nickname for president of Belarus <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alyaksandr_Lukashenka" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alyaksandr Lukashenka">Alyaksandr Lukashenka</a>, also the Belarusian term <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">ба́цька</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bácʹka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used in this sense.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батя.html>ба́тя</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bátja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батенька.html>ба́тенька</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bátenʹka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батюшка.html>ба́тюшка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bátjuška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ба́тько</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bátʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>/<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">батько́</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">batʹkó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">батя́ня</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">batjánja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***батя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:батя.html>ба́тя</a> (6552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">батѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">batę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*batę</i>, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">баща́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baštá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Alternatively from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*brat(r)ъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батя.html>ба́тя</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bátja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батя.html>ба́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батя.html>ба́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:батя.html>ба́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dad</li>
<li><i>familiar term of address for an elderly man</i></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">baule</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баул.html>бау́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">baúl</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баул.html>бау́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баул.html>бау́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баул.html>бау́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>portmanteau</li>
<li>trunk, a large travel bag</li></ol>

<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="историческое">истор.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:турецкий.html>туре́цких</a> иррегулярных <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йск</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:пеший.html>пеший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a>) XVIII—XIX <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>веко́в</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:заметить.html>заме́ть</a>, Веруня, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:башибузук.html>башибузу́ки</a></span> вырезывали <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пикет.html>пике́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ярославский.html>яросла́вская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огород.html>огоро́де</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:срезать.html>среза́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:капустный.html>капу́стные</a> кочни. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%9A%D1%83%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B8%D0%BD,_%D0%90%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B4%D1%80_%D0%98%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Куприн, Александр Иванович"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a>. ***башка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:башка.html>башка</a> (4014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language, probably a borrowing of a dative singular form attested in Kipchak languages; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href = vnd.unilang:баш.html>баш</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baş</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bashkir_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bashkir language">Bashkir</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ba">башҡа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ba-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bašqa</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head.1SG.DAT</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Initial (in 17th century) meaning 'head of a large fish' implies an origin related to fish trade in South Russia (e.g. on Volga and Don).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башка.html>башка́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bašká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башка.html>башки́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башка.html>башки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башка.html>башо́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pate, noggin, bonce (slang word for head, part of the body)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подумать.html>поду́май</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:башка.html>башко́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:последствие.html>после́дствиях</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Podúmaj svojéj <b>baškój</b> o poslédstvijax!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Use your <b>noggin</b>, think of the consequences!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:баш.html>баш</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> ненормативный <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 3*d <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чередование.html>чередова́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ве</a>: мн. ч. <i>бо́шки, бо́шек, бо́шкам, бо́шками, бо́шках</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:либо.html>ли́бо</a> 3*d' — <a href = vnd.unilang:дополнительный.html>дополни́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. ед. <i>бо́шку</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-башк-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.

***башмак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башма́к</a> (3773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from  a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source. 
Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башма́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">başmaq</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shoe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">başmak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shoe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башма́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bašmák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башмака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башмаки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башмако́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shoe</li>
<li>boot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:башмак.html>башмако́м</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ pod <b>bašmakóm</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be henpecked</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>chock</li></ol>

***башня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шня</a> (2114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First recorded in the 1st Pskov manuscript. Often used in the 17th century. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">башта</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bašta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">bastia</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">baszta</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">bašta</i>. The ending was influenced by the suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which creates nouns of place, as in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пашня.html>па́шня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pášnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таможня.html>тамо́жня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tamóžnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bášnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tower
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вавилонский.html>вавило́нская</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vavilónskaja <b>bášnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <b>tower</b> of Babel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">водонапо́рная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodonapórnaja <b>bášnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">water tower</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">э́йфелева <a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шня</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éjfeleva bášnja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Eiffel Tower</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шня</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слоновый.html>слоно́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>ко́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bášnja</b> iz slonóvoj kósti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ivory tower</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>turret
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожевой.html>сторожева́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">storoževája <b>bášnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">watchtower</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***баян.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баян.html>бая́н</a> (12367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The “old joke” sense originated from a joke (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_meme" class="extiw" title="w:Internet meme">Internet meme</a>) at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.anekdot.ru">http://www.anekdot.ru</a> — "<a href = vnd.unilang:хоронить.html>Хорони́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теща.html>тёщу</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баян.html>бая́на</a>" (when we buried my mother-in-law, we broke two accordions).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баян.html>бая́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">baján</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баян.html>бая́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баян.html>бая́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баян.html>бая́нов</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бдеть.html>бдеть</a> (25437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бъдѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bŭděti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be awake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъděti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be awake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*bud-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰudʰ</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бдеть.html>бдеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bdetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be awake, not sleep

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep watch, to keep vigil</li></ol>

***бдительность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бдительность.html>бди́тельность</a> (7622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бдительный.html>бди́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bdítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бдительность.html>бди́тельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bdítelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бдительность.html>бди́тельности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бдительность.html>бди́тельности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бдительность.html>бди́тельностей</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бег.html>бега́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">begá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бег.html>бего́в</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>races, horse-race</li>
<li>hiding
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бег.html>бега́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ v begáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be on the run, to be in hiding, to be outlawed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бегать</a> (1328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*běgati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰegʷ-</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">bėgti</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">φέβομαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phébomai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bégatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побегать.html>побе́гать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побегать.html>побе́гать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are abstract verbs. Their counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побежать.html>побежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pobežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.</li>
<li>The compounds of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></b> are formed from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бега́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-begátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<ol><li>runaway, fugitive</li>
<li>jailbreaker</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">béglyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегло.html>бе́гло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">béglo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fluently <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">expressing oneself easily</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бегло.html>бе́гло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>béglo</b> čitátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read fluently</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>superficially, cursorily
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бегло.html>бе́гло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:просмотреть.html>просмотре́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>béglo</b> prosmotrétʹ knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to glance over / through a book</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глый</a> (24315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">béglyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fluent, quick, fast</li>
<li>superficial, cursory</li>
<li>fugitive</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">béglyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глых</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беглый.html>бе́глая</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fugitive</li></ol>

***беда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беда</a> (1184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*běda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰeydʰ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bide</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">faith</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fidelity</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bedá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>бе́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>бе́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>misfortune, trouble, disaster, mischief</li></ol>

***бедлам.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бедлам.html>бедла́м</a> (29733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедлам.html>бедла́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bedlám</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедлам.html>бедла́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедлам.html>бедла́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бедлам.html>бедла́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bedlam <i>(alternative name to Bethlem)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religious</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hell, afterlife</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chaos, madhouse</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>бе́д</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лама.html>ла́м</a></b>
